 **Table of contents**
 
 .. contents::
    :local:
 
 Usage
 =====
 
 To create a new state:
 
-#. Go to *Sales > Configuration > Products > Product States*.
-#. You can set its name and a description.
+1. Go to *Sales > Configuration > Products > Product States*.
+2. You can set its name and a description.
 
 To add a product to a state:
 
-#. Go to the product itself and edit.
-#. You can select the desired status in the list of buttons above the form.
+1. Go to the product itself and edit.
+2. You can select the desired status in the list of buttons above the
+   form.

 Usage
 =====
 
 To create a new state:
 
-#. Go to *Sales > Configuration > Products > Product States*.
-#. You can set its name and a description.
+1. Go to *Sales > Configuration > Products > Product States*.
+2. You can set its name and a description.

-#. Go to the product itself and edit.
-#. You can select the desired status in the list of buttons above the form.
+1. Go to the product itself and edit.
+2. You can select the desired status in the list of buttons above the
+   form.
